Sugar Beet and Man Bun

Two Sydney Office Turds Keeping Australia Great Again by Doing Absolutely Nothing at All


Man Bun: The way of showing the world you are a turds without having to speak. Also known as a Douche Donut.

— urbandictionary.com

Sugar Beet (Beta vulgaris): A sugar beet is a plant whose root contains a high concentration of sucrose and which is grown commercially for sugar production.

— wikipedia.org


I do not document the activities of party actors. I never indulge in that mundane form of demeaning theatrics. Individual human beings and their personalities interest me not, and nor do their politics. People and their petty concerns bore me to the core. Humanity’s been done to death. Just read any random selection of novels written by any other author after Defoe and you’ll quickly come to understand what I mean. However, given my current state of extreme irritation, and the extreme nature of the circumstances that brought this state about, on just this one occasion am I left with no alternative other than to indulge. So indulge I shall.

Now, it should come as no great surprise at this stage in my life that I have plainly run out of patience with your blatant inefficiency in the workplace. I simply cannot tolerate it any longer. I have no time for your juvenile antics and mindless apathy, your endless malingering and inane chitchat, your petty rivalries and salacious intrigues, your sexual predation and egregious abuses of power – and nor do you. I’m putting an end to it all right now. For let it be known henceforth that I refuse to suffer any longer the vile tyranny of infantile office turds. No longer shall I remain silent. Now, shall I denounce and revile them all!

I shall begin with Sugar Beet. Let me just say, first off, that I love the English, I really do – cricket, crumpets, Earl Grey Tea, the BBC, etc. So it really does pain me to acknowledge the fact that the same brand of benighted peasantry that exists all over the world also exists in England. This acknowledgement, brought about by a “chance” encounter with the one I refer to as Sugar Beet (or Lord Beetly, or Mister Beets, whichever you prefer), and patently realised whilst prostrating myself yet again before the sacred altar of the Holy Church of Corporate Whorism, brought forth within me such an overwhelming sense of resentment that I can barely even begin to comprehend the sense of it myself, let alone express it in written form. So I’ll instead move on to Man Bun.

Man Bun, the skinny jean-wearing, man-bunned fascist jewboy from Melbourne, is a much simpler proposition. I can characterise Man Bun with a single phrase: “I’m not a coffee drinker.” I must have overheard him say this at least five or six times in the course of a week, and he would always say it with such a heightened sense of moral tenor during conversations that had nothing to do with coffee. I’m sorry, but that just really irritated me. I mean whoever heard of a dev from Melbourne who doesn’t drink coffee? It just doesn’t sit right, does it? No. Because he’s not really a dev and he’s not really from Melbourne, and he’s probably not even Jewish. He’s just an idiotic office turd and a terrible actor. And no, I’m not a raging anti-Semite. Please do keep in mind that I am the literary heir of Anne Frank and forever wed to the ghost of Franz Kafka...at least in my own mind.

Now, I don’t know if you’ve ever been sugar-beeted or man-bunned in the workplace before, but I’d be willing to wager the vast majority of you have, so you probably understand exactly how I feel right now – and if you don’t now, you will soon enough. What’s the right word for that feeling? That “fuck you” kind of feeling? It’s a feeling I can only express verbally by resorting to the very basest form of coinage: FUCKYOUITY or FUCKUITY. I shall accept either variant. In any case, I’m sure you all know what I’m talking about.

And I’m sure, too, that you are all well aware that I have now reached a state of absolute peak fuckuity. The absolute peak occurred while Sugar Beet and Man Bun were discussing the burning issues of our time over a two-hour Darling Harbour lunch: “What’s the difference between agnostic and the Gnostics? And weren’t the Gnostics really just Islamic fundamentalist scholars in disguise who secretly plotted the destruction of European civilization?” After a few minutes pondering the absolute absurdity of this conversation, and then pondering for a few minutes more the equal absurdity of my current state in the world, I suddenly rose, excused myself and went outside for a smoke. Whilst attempting to gaze out across the harbour, a thought suddenly occurred to me that had never occurred before: It is no mere coincidence that the redundancy of humanity and the ruination of the Earth have coincided at this precise moment in history. That’s called an epiphany, is it not?

Thank you, Sugar Beet and Man Bun, for showing me the True Way to The Absolute Greatness of Nothing.

I now leave you to your sugar-beeting man-bunned fate, Sydney. I’m defecting to lutruwita.

Fuck you.

Rare Penguin Appears

This Fjordland penguin was a rare sight on Granite Island last week.

Standing at twice the size of the fairy penguins, around 50-60cm tall, and weighing in at two to three kilograms, the bird attracted a lot of attention.

Native to New Zealand, the penguin is believed to have travelled the vast distance from its homeland on ocean currents.

Les McDiarmid, of the SA Whale Centre said the bird had been disturbed slightly on the island as it began its moulting period.

National Parks and Wildlife officers captured the bird and relocated it to West Island so it could carry out this moulting stage in peace.


— Victor Harbour Times (31 Jan, 1995)

Open Letter to Prime Lump

Dear Prime Lump,

I am writing to you today to express my sincere shock and dismay at just how dodgy you are. You’re just so fucking dodgy, mate, it’s not fucking funny. I mean seriously, what the fuck is going on? Why are you so fucking dodgy, mate?

I’m sorry, but I really don’t think I can continue this relationship if all I get from you is constant fucking dodginess. Therefore, I must inform you that unless you consent to a full and detailed audit on just how dodgy you are, this relationship must and will come to an end.

Your audit begins on the 1st of May, 2020 at 00:00 UTC.

And on second thought, your consent is not required.

No doubt you are curious as to what precipitated such a decisive resolution to conduct such an extensive audit of your extreme dodginess? I need only mention the following, all of which I have experienced while living and working in your nation’s capital:

Exploitive landlords who steal your mail, spy on you and refuse to return your bond; workplace stalkers and all those flattering fawners and malignant misinformers; oafish office chatbots who deliberately go out of their way to disrupt their colleagues by chatting for hours on end about non-work-related topics no one else cares about but themselves; devious and small-minded social-climbing wannabe politicians, and their sycophantic self-serving supporters; mob boss building managers and their hired goons who run the parking extortion rackets, and who assault you in the lift if you refuse to pay to park in the same building you work; and public service parasites who openly scam the government with impunity, while their feckless enablers turn a blind eye and feign ignorance.

More broadly, you’re fucking burning us all to death, you fucking fuckwit!

I ask you plainly, is not all this more than enough to fully warrant such a resolution? Seriously, how can I get any work done with all this dodginess going on? And how can I live and breath with all this constant fucking smoke in the air?

Our legal representatives will contact you within the next ten days to familiarise you with the preliminary proceedings and explain to you your legal rights and obligations.

Yours faithfully,

Some dude who just wants to live and work without all the dodginess.

Update: You’re no longer Prime Lump, and the damage is already done. And I’m no longer an Australian, so none of this matters anymore.

- The Minds and Movement of Sheep, and their Shit

I now live alone in a cosy little cottage on a sheep shit farm in the Valley of Yass. My only friends are the sheep, and their shit. For I tend to think of the sheep more as my fellow farm-dwelling friends rather than as mere sheep (despite their shit), and I’m pretty sure they think the same way of me. There’s really not too much difference between a human being and a sheep anyway, existentially speaking. Yet despite this spirit of inter-species pastoral fellowship, this idyllic relationship has come under some strain of late. For you see not all is quite as it seems with my seemingly quaint ovine acquaintances. My relationship with one sheep in particular, for whom I have now reserved an unreserved antipathy, is primarily responsible for this increased level of strain. This Demon Sheep, as I have dubbed her, has a ponderously deep and resoundingly sonorous bah. (Over the last few months I have learned to differentiate individual sheep and identify them by the pitch and timbre of their distinctive bahs.) Unearthly and unsettling it is. I find it impossible not to imitate whenever she is near. This never fails to irritate her greatly. I can tell by the way her demonic grey sheep eyes narrow and fix me with concentrated disdain whenever I am near. Why do I delight in tormenting the poor beast so? I know I shouldn’t, yet I cannot help myself. Bahahaha!

In short, this Demon Sheep doesn’t like me very much. And because she’s the matriarch of all the sheep, now all the other sheep don’t like me much either. The other problem is their shit. It’s everywhere. I should have known that would be the case before deciding to live on a sheep shit farm, that much is true. But I didn’t expect it to be everywhere. In some places, under the pine trees for instance, the ground beneath is nothing but a thick dense layer of highly compacted sheep shit. As I’m sure you can appreciate, the odour, especially when it rains, is not a very pleasant one.

They say “human beings are biohazards, machines are not”. Are sheep? They eat their own shit. The earth is caked with it and there’s not much else to eat. Isn’t that how mad cow disease first got started, when people started feeding the same animal back to itself? I wonder how flammable their shit is.

Not that I’m here to do a jolly jumbuck or anything. What do I care if all the sheep hate me? Fuck sheep. What do I care about them? They eat their own shit.

And then I met Ovis, which complicated matters even further. Ovis (full name Ovis Aries) is simply the sweetest and most darling little lamb one could ever hope to lay eyes on. I saw him frolicking about in the south field one day, his pristine white fleece shining in the noonday sun, his high-pitched rollicking bahs echoing joyously throughout the valley, his curly woolly fringe bobbing up and down adorably above his rather distinctive human-like eyes. What can I say? I was immediately smitten. Yes, by a sheep. But then Ovis is no mere sheep. Ovis is the apotheosis of all sheep. The perfect sheep! For Ovis truly is every best bit of a sheep imaginable, in every respect and in all proportions – if not, according to some, for his one most obvious defect. According to them, his eyes look like they were cut out of a 1980s fashion magazine and hastily pasted on upside down and too far apart. I must admit, they kind of do. But in my eyes Ovis is still perfectly adorable, including his eyes. I simply couldn’t imagine Ovis with any other set of eyes other than those he was born with, however oddly shaped and ill-positioned they admittedly may be.

However that may be, my affection for Ovis complicates matters even further not just because Ovis is a sheep, but also because Ovis just happens to be the son of the Demon Sheep. The resemblance could not be less striking. Prodigious birth of love it is to me that I must love a loathed enemy. In light of this knowledge, I am now at once forced to reassess my relationship with not only The Demon Sheep but with all of ovine kind. Thus, you’ll be happy to learn, my feeling of unreserved antipathy towards the Demon Sheep, and thus all sheep in general, is presently undergoing a close and much needed reexamination.

At this point I must also introduce Farmer Rob. And yes, his name really is Rob. Farmer Rob is your typical salt of the earth conservative Christian farmer type in his mid 70s. Yes, they still exist. He owns all of Merryvale Estates, the official name Farmer Rob has given to his sheep shit farm. Back when Farmer Rob inherited the land – 250 hectares of what may have been prime grazing land at some point in time – it was simply known as the “Merry Farm”. But now, now that it’s so dry, and now that the entire farm is covered with sheep shit, Farmer Rob has since been forced to diversify away from sheep into the real estate industry. For $500 a week you too can live on a sheep shit farm, all alone in a cosy little asbestos-lined cottage, furnished with nothing but a small wood-burning “low combustion” fireplace and surrounded by nothing but sheep shit and pine trees for miles and miles around. But act now! This offer won’t last long. It won’t be too much longer now before the encroaching suburban sprawl surrounding the Yass Valley township reaches the margins of Merryvale Estates, inevitably forcing Farmer Rob to cash in big time by selling out to speculative property developers. I wonder what he’ll spend the money on. Will he buy a huge luxury yacht, a polyester polo shirt, some orthopaedic sandals and retire to Port Douglas? Or will he immigrate to Israel and use his hard-earned cash to reinvest in the real estate industry over there? Jerusalem perhaps? One can only speculate.

I don’t mean to sound as though I bear any ill will towards Farmer Rob. I’m merely stating the facts of the matter and conservatively speculating on their potential outcomes. Although, I must admit I did have a rather disconcerting altercation with Farmer Rob just recently which has somewhat degraded my opinion of him of late. We had a falling out after he kept demanding I mow my lush green lawn – the very same lawn I fully restored to a lush green state from the dry and barren wasteland I inherited when I first arrived (at my own expense and labour, I might add). He’s even started stopping by my cottage every day to check on my lush green lawn and see if I’ve mowed it yet. I haven’t. Then, yesterday, when he stopped by yet again, and after repeatedly promising on previous surprise inspections that I’d mow it as soon as possible, I finally reconciled with my conscience and straight out refused him. You’re only supposed to mow the same patch of grass twice a year anyway. I forget what I said to him exactly, but I don’t believe the manner in which I expressed my recusant intent was in any way rude or impolite. Nonetheless, Farmer Rob became extremely irate upon learning of my open defiance of his extremist lawn care dictates. He even had the temerity to threaten me with a quaint array of colonial-era expletives, while his face turned an alarming shade of firehouse red and his beady little eyes bulged out of his archaic hoary head. That’s when I too became extremely irate and fired off a few expletives of my own. I shouted at him that he was clearly a stupid old evil cunt and in future to stay the fuck away from me. Ping, one of Farmer Rob’s faceporn-order child brides, was with him that day. She’s the one who told me about the Demon Sheep being Ovis’ mother. I always get along well with Ping. Of all Farmer Rob’s faceporn-order child brides (Pong and Pang being the others), Ping is certainly the most subversive and the easiest to talk to. I attribute this, in part, to her being a fellow starving artist (of sorts). Ping likes to paint highly abstract expressionist water colours of sheep in her spare time. She’s the one who also told me, shortly after my altercation with Farmer Rob, that I should perhaps consider vacating my cosy little cottage and leaving the Valley of Yass, never to return.

I’ve never once felt at ease in the Valley of Yass. Granted, my feelings for this particular region of Australia have been very much negatively inflected by all the psychological trauma I’ve suffered of late at the hands of Farmer Rob and his Demon Sheep, while living all alone in abject isolation on a sheep shit farm, that much is true. Yet there’s also the knowledge that this particular region of Australia does have a rather dark and disturbing past. They used to call it Ngunnawal country, now they call it Hume country (Yass) – named after Hamilton Hume (1797-1873) the Scottish-Australian overland explorer and master land thief, not David Hume (1711-1776) the Scottish-English philosopher and antiquated British historian. Hamilton Hume’s Wikipedia page is one of the most boring I’ve ever read. I won’t bore you, therefore, any more than is strictly necessary with the boring details of his boring life. Enough to state that 200 years ago Hamilton Hume rode an ass from Melbourne to Sydney, passing through Ngunnawal country as he did so and illegally taking possession of a vast tract of newly rediscovered land he called The Valley of Yass, and that “Yass” is derived from an Aboriginal word, Yarrh or Yharr, said to mean running water. Hume added the “ass”. He was somewhat hard of hearing.

There’s not too much running water around here nowadays. Back in Hume’s time, however, this particular region of Australia, although still quite dry, was one of the most verdant and fertile. The Yass river, as it is known today, flowed wild and free through the valley in those days (a far cry from the foul and pestilent, carp-infested effluential discharge of a shit stream that it is today). Many sacred old trees lined the banks of the river back then, and beyond them lush green pastures as far as the eye could see. Kangaroos, emus, countless species of birds and insects, all thrived in this region once. Not so today. Now there’s nothing but people and sheep, and their shit. But back then The Valley of Yass was a pastoralist’s paradise. From the moment he first laid eyes on the place Hume knew this is where he would live out the end of his days.

Of course, Hume never really “discovered” the Valley of Yass. This region of Australia, like most regions of Australia, had already been inhabited by human beings for tens of thousands of years. The Valley of Yass was revealed to Hume by a local large-breasted fourteen-year-old Aboriginal woman named Jin. Jin, constantly drunk and half-blind from all the smallpox blisters that covered her entire face, gracefully guided Hume and his ass over The Overlands to their final destination. (“The Overlands” is what they used to call the land between Melbourne and Sydney back then.) They experienced many hardships along the way. It rained a lot and Hume ran out of tobacco around Lake George. They did have plenty of gin, however. And yet the gin in no way impeded their progress. They walked barefoot all the way from Melbourne to Sydney in six days. Well, Jin walked, Hume rode his ass (while smoking his pipe). They also stopped for one day in what is now known as The Valley of Yass – so Hume could illegally take possession of it. (Most of the original inhabitants were already dead from smallpox by then anyway.) It was the river that sold Hume on the place. Upon arriving at the banks of the River of Yass Hume is said to have dropped to his knees, raised his arms in praise and exclaimed “Now am I come unto the Valley of Yass where the waters of life flow wild and free! Here shall I guide my flock and build my cottage.” Jin tried on many occasions to correct Hume’s gross mispronunciation of the name of her ancestral homelands – all to no avail. She also tried to talk him out of importing thousands of sheep into the area, also to no avail. Just before he died Hume tended over 60,000 head of sheep, and he still pronounced the word Yarrh as “Yass”. Moreover, in his latter years Hume became increasingly paranoid it would become widely known that Jin was the true leader of their expedition. A few weeks before he died Hume took to pacing around fully naked in one of his four kitchens for hours on end while nervously muttering to himself revised phrases from his grand “Statement” (A Brief Statement of Facts in Connection with an Overland Expedition from Melbourne to Sydney Undertaken Alone and Unaided by Hamilton Hume in the Year 1824 with No One Else’s Assistance, Guidance or Advice Whatsoever). Would he ever finish it? Right up until the moment of his death this remained his most pressing concern. One of his most respected and authoritative biographers sums up the end of Hume’s life in similar terms:


Almost totally deaf, with a failing memory, and now obsessed with the idea that his place in the 1824 expedition had not been restored in the public’s estimation, he was preparing a second edition of his Statement when he died at his home, Cooma Cottage, Yass, on 19 April 1873.

— A respected and authoritative biographer of Hamilton Hume


Cooma Cottage is just down the road from Merryvale Estates. I’ve never visited the property myself (it’s been closed to the public since Covid started), but I’ve driven past it many times. Not that I ever take any notice. You can’t see it from the road anyway. From what I’ve read about the place, however, it does sound like quite the swanky residence. The word cottage is, of course, misleading. It is in truth more a stately country mansion – a superb example of Australian colonial-era Palladian-homestead architecture, with a vast and imposing main entrance, over 20 tastefully decorated guest rooms, four kitchens, a well-stocked wine cellar and a swimming pool on the second floor. Cooma Cottage is indeed an eminently suitable ancestral rural seat and an iconic architectural monument to the much celebrated Overland exploring legacy of Hamilton Hume, may his land thieving ass rest in peace.

No one knows what happened to Jin. But it is known that Jin left Hume shortly after they moved in together at Cooma Cottage. She ran off to Singapore with a handsome young chimney sweep named Sean. Jin just couldn’t stand all the sheep, and their shit. Not only that, the stables were bitterly cold in the winter and the daily rapes and beatings were becoming quite brutal. Hume was devastated. But eventually he found another wife (also named Jin). No great loss there. Jin was never really into Hume to begin with. She merely considered him a bridge to a somewhat better life and as a safeguard against getting raped and beaten by other men (again). Then there was the gin. Hume always had plenty of gin, and Jin liked drinking plenty of gin. They actually met at a gin joint, in Cooma. Bernie’s Gin Joint they called it back then. Jin was working there as a barmaid with her friend, also named Jin. Jin was already seven months pregnant from a previous rape when she met Hume. He just walked straight up to her one day at work and asked if she was from The Overlands. When Jin indicated that she was indeed from The Overlands (Ngunnawal Country), Hume went on to explain that he was in need of a guide, as he was soon setting forth on an expedition over The Overlands. Payment would consist of a blanket and a bottle of gin – plus all the gin one could care to drink during the expedition. After much deliberation, and after getting Hume to throw in another bottle of gin, Jin gladly accepted Hume’s offer. She was headed back that way anyway to give birth.

And Jin did indeed give birth in The Valley of Yass. While Hume was on his knees giving praise to the waters of life by the river that day, Jin quietly slipped off into the bushes. After disposing of the fetus – by burying it under a large stone by the side of the river – she then quietly staggered off to get another bottle of gin. She still had a piece of rope between her teeth as she emerged from the bushes.

But that’s enough about the dark and disturbing past of this particular region of Australia. I’m sure I’ve bored you all enough as it is – much more so than is strictly necessary. There is, needless to say, so much more to tell regarding the dark and disturbing past of the Valley of Yass. But to be honest, most of it’s terribly uninteresting. In any case, I’m not a historian, and Australian history really is the surest way to put a reader to sleep.

But at least you now know why they named that highway between Melbourne and Sydney the Hume Highway.


Hume : 1: Scottish (Lowlands) and northern English: variant of Hulme with loss of l before the bilabial consonant m as in the vocabulary word calm. See Holm and Home. 2: Scottish: habitational name either from the barony of Home or from Hume (or Home) in Berwickshire from which the barony took its name. The placename derives from Old English hōum dative plural form of hōh ‘heel spur of land’.

— geneanet.org

Interlude One: Lycidas and The Fates, and The Mystic Lamb

The Fates: Where is your Philomela, Lycidas?

Lycidas: ‘Where there is leisure for fiction there is little grief.’ My Philomela is dead. You killed her.

The Fates: Ever wonder why The Fates are plural?

Lycidas: Yes, I have. The Furies too.

And The Mystic Lamb turned to me with tears in his ungodly eyes and said, Hic est fons aque vite procendens de sede Dei + Agni.. And the words echoed throughout the valley.

And then I heard a thunderous voice in the heavens say “Now it is time. Bring him to me. We must dehumanise the lamb once more!”

Lycidas: It’s always fascinating to see how the cultivated, in their artificial way, reflect upon and describe, for their own ends, the natural life.

The Mystic Lamb: Hic est fons aque vite procendens de sede Dei + Agni.

They say the literal translation of Hic est fons aque vite procendens de sede Dei + Agni. is “This is the fountain of the water of life, proceeding out of the throne of God and the Lamb.” I don’t know about that. But I do know that I hate irony, and a contemplation of the waters of life mythos right now could hardly be thought of as anything less than perfect irony. Besides, I have a low combustion fireplace to keep.

Now am I honestly divorced from humanity. Only after a clean break and after demolishing some compromised structures to halt the destructive front can we begin to prevent the spread.


Interlude Two: The Ghost of Jack the Anarchist

The man known to history as Jack the Anarchist never actually existed. He was entirely fabricated by the Australian branch of the CIA – as too was his ghost. Ghosts don’t exist either.

But they say Jack the Anarchist lived in Quaama, a small town in the South Coast region of New South Wales. So I took a drive out to Quaama yesterday. I even drove past what I imagined to be the burnt out remains of Jack’s home. And that’s where I saw The Ghost of Jack the Anarchist.

I drove south, across the “snowy” ridge that divides cow from sheep – one side all burnt away, the other side all blown away – and then from Cobargo to Quaama, through the incinerated remains of what was once one half of the Murramarang National Park, then back up through the Valley of Yass. I witnessed appalling scenes of unimaginable devastation along the way. The haunting grandeur of what was once one half of the Murramarang National Park is now nothing more than... [orange tops. something else to link it back to pine plantations and McDonald's signs unscathed.].

Well, I’m here to tell you that Jack the Anarchist did actually exist. I saw his his ghost.

Drove past a few charred dead koala bears by the side of the road. ...[]

And then I began to believe I was Lord Vervex again.

Bush fires of unprecedented scale and ferocity, thick choking smoke, gale force winds and blinding dust storms, and then giant hail stones and torrential rain for two days straight, and then a great plague of mass-suicidal flying insects (most of which ended up dead on my kitchen floor), and now yet another dust storm, and that ingrate of a spider that bit my finger when I caught and released it to the great outdoors, all within the last two months. Oh, and now a deadly global pandemic. What’s next, I wonder?

Fuck sheep and fuck pine trees too. And now they’ve fucked up the land so much so they’re all switching to goats crossbred with alpacas and a new genetically engineered species of South Saharan sedge. Like they haven’t fucked it up enough.

Sheep bleat contentedly in oblivious chorus; crows caw with ominous intent in contrapuntal accompaniment; pine needles whistle in the wind like millions of miniature jet engines.

Who would have thought a deadly global pandemic combined with a few hundred devastating megafires and the rise of ultranationalist authoritarianism all over the world could become so disruptive?

But no need to panic just yet. They cut down all the trees here long ago (but for the pine trees), and the global Covid death toll is still only around 7,000 people per day (so they say).

If worst comes to worst I suppose I can always get some chickens and grow my own vegetables. I just wish I knew how to weave and bake bread. I may have to buy a big basket and start stockpiling wholegrain English muffins.

Human beings are just so completely insane. Seriously, plenty of everything else on the shelves but no toilet paper. What’s so special about toilet paper, Farmer Rob? You can’t eat it, you know. Who killed my dear sweet Ovis? Was it really the Mexican asparagus? Or was his death meant as a warning? Did Farmer Rob intentionally sacrifice the first lamb of his flock for me?

The Uncouth Swain within emerges. A wildly swung blunt hatchet and then a slow loving lambaste over the open fires of direct retribution.

Perhaps it is indeed time for me to leave the Valley of Yass, never to return.

The rains come and the valley greens. The skies clear, momentarily. A few days pass, any memory of which has also since passed. Time annihilates all, even memory. Poor Ovis.

I’m listening to the Agnus Dei from Bach’s Mass in B minor. The sun is setting across the valley. Qui tollis pecata mundi. Now it’s dark. I can see both the large and small Brolga galaxies (large and small Magellanic clouds) with my naked eye from my front yard. Barefoot and heavily pregnant, standing on a lush green lawn while gazing up at the stars – principally, the Mars, Jupiter and Saturn conjunction in Sagittarius. Yes, at the very least am I now blessed with heavy impregnation and lawn barefootedness.

Quite a frosty morning. Why am I always waking up at 4AM? It rained last night and the fire went out again, and I’ve run out chopped firewood. I have to chop the tree trunk-sized hardwood logs they use for firewood around here into at least quarters to get them to burn. I fetch a damp unchopped log from outside and throw it into the smouldering ashes. It won’t burn. My log will not burn and my muffin will not defrost!

It’s now half an hour later. Half a box of firelighters and a generous splash of lawnmower fuel solved my no combustion fireplace issues. Now I’m buttering my muffin. Poor Ovis.

Now I’m eating my muffin, while gazing up at the fading stars. All is silent, but for the words of the Mystic Lamb, which keep echoing through my mind.

Aries rises before the dawn as I eat my muffin in silence and think of Ovis.

And still the words of the Mystic Lamb keep echoing through my mind:

Hic est fons aque vite procendens de sede Dei + Agni.

The Valley of Yass, Australia, 2020

The Day the Wind Blew the Door Off My Chicken Coop

The Day the wind blew the door of my chicken coop I was making my second most favourite dish for dinner: Penang gai kai dao mai sook. I was so distraught I wrote a little poem about it seven days later:

The door flew off my chicken coop;
The wind blew it off it did.
It’s been that way for a week now.
Good thing I don’t have any chickens.

I’ve been meaning to get me some chickens, once I get around to fixing the door on my chicken coop. But I’m afraid if I do they’ll all get blown away. I’m also afraid I just won’t be able to enjoy my second-most favourite dish again in quite the same way.

Horse Eats Man (or Never Buy Weed in Bondi)

I used to buy weed from a racist old white fella in Bondi with a pathological fear of horses. On more than one occasion, and with a look of sincere terror in his pale grey eyes, he would tell me of how when he was a child back in Tasmania a horse once tried to eat him. His mother had taken him to visit some friends who lived on a stud farm. He was feeding a big black horse some hay when suddenly the horse lunged forward and clenched him by the groin. The horse shook him violently to and fro, hurling him six feet into the air. He landed face down, writhing in agony, in a huge pile of horse shit.

I guess even horses hate racists.

The surf conditions weren’t great that day, but there was no one on the beach anyway. All the restaurants, pubs and shops were shut and the streets deserted. It was wonderful. I’d been to Bondi Beach many times before, but only now could I really begin to appreciate the true appeal of the place. I closed my eyes. Nothing but the sound of the wind and the waves. Wonderful.

Forgive me, I’m usually not much of a beach person. The truly iconic Australian cultural experience of bronzed burly blokes in skimpy speedos passing line over their heads and willingly showering with one another has never much appealed to me. However truly egalitarian and enjoyable that experience may still yet be, I still much prefer the highlands.

So why travel over 600 kilometres from your home in the highlands to Bondi and back every weekend just to buy weed when most of it’s grown in the highlands?

Good question.

There are five principle reasons:

  1. At the time of writing, the cultivation of marijuana for personal use is still illegal in New South Wales. The possession of marijuana for personal use is illegal too, but a lesser offence and usually overlooked.
  2. Although most marijuana is grown in the highlands, I just don’t know anyone in the highlands who grows marijuana – besides my next-door neighbour. But he kind of looks like that Hans Klopeck dude from that 80s Tom Hanks movie The Burbs, so I don’t talk to him.
  3. Bondi Beach is a heavily touristed area, and wherever there is a beach and a preponderance of tourism there are dealers – and I just don’t trust the “dark web” or “crypto”.
  4. Despite being a racist and a stalker, and a probable ex-rapist, my Bondi marijuana dealer is a cat lover and in most other respects a relatively okay “bloke”. And despite the quality of the product, and the price, I was more than willing to suffer the indignity of associating with him – if only for the purpose of completing this piece.
  5. I don’t really get out of the house much nowadays, so a nice long drive through the New South Wales semi-rural-industrialised countryside, even if it is to Sydney, comes as a welcome break from the menial weekday monotony of staying in all day and doing fuck all, even if it is during a deadly global pandemic. I also take advantage of the six-hour drive there and back to brush up on my country music knowledge.

Some Tom Hanks militarist propaganda “movie” about whacking African fishermen-cum-pirates is playing on the television as I enter his cramped yet cosy abode. He always greets me with an air of fake bemused surprise, as though he has no forewarning of my arrival, then directs me through to the area where he entertains his guests. After dispensing with the usual formalities of initial reacquaintance, and after enduring a cursory and conspiracy-laden lecture on all manner of diverse topics – from the looming and inevitable war with China, to how an intense increase in the Earth’s gravitational field was the true cause of the extinction of the dinosaurs – and after petting his cat and throwing in a few humouring or corrective comments of my own, inevitability, and without fail, he always betrays his deeply ingrained racism by making some highly insensitive and factually inaccurate comment regarding migrant or indigenous communities. It is then that I excuse myself and depart.

I’m riding my silver pony along the prairie and stopping just before the Chain of Ponds cross road to take a leak. I think back to Book VII of Aristotle’s Metaphysics:


If ‘animal’ is one and the same thing in ‘horse’ and in ‘man’, in just the same way that you are the same thing as yourself, how can this one thing that in things that are apart be one?

We are both “man”, yet you are a racist and I am not. We may just as well be different species. Perhaps there’s some truth to that. Perhaps they are all “genetic” racists, as they so often claim is true of all of “man” (and anyone who denies this is a hypocrite of course). And so, in effect, psycho-biologically at least, racists are a different species of human? Homo non sapiens, perhaps? Does that not call into question the very question of what it means to be human? You see, my friend? If I choose to misapply the same rudimentary logic you employ, we could all end up in a very difficult situation.

As I repackage my equipment and remount my diminutive steed, a favourite Jimmie Rodgers tune, Prairie Lullaby, suddenly pops into my head:


Saddle up your pony
The sandman’s here
To guide you down the trail of dreams...

Jimmie was probably a racist too, but at least he wrote some good shit.

Note: Billy Hill wrote Prairie Lullaby, not Jimmie Rodgers.

With one of the most wonderfully serene scenes of proto-post-industrialised Australiana I have ever beheld – the clean white sands of a totally deserted Bondi Beach impressed firmly into my long-term memory – and with the Meriton-dominated skyline of greater metropolitan Sydney receding in my rear view mirror, I shifted my little Hyundai into fifth gear, breathed a deep sigh of palliative relief, tuned out on some Jimmie Rodgers and trundled on down the Hume highway back to my humble home in the highlands. I timed the drive precisely so as to catch the last few hours of late afternoon sunshine and arrive back just before dark – and also so I could watch the sun set through the clouds over Lake George (Weereewa). “Lake George”, right. They call it a lake and named it after George Orwell, but it’s not really a lake. It’s a vast floodplain that very rarely fully floods – yet when it does flood it does so catastrophically. I call it the Valley of Nothing. You must pass through the Valley of Nothing to pass through the Valley of Yass, unless you take the Federal Highway turn-off, in which case you must still pass through the Valley of Nothing.

I decided to pass through the Valley of Yass, not taking the federal highway turn-off, because Canberra is just that. I was pulled over by the speed police upon entering the Valley of Yass. Downhill straight stretch. I usually only speed around corners and up hills. I was a little over the speed limit, I admit. But it was a pleasant evening, and I’m white, so he let me off with a warning. Praise the LORD for social distancing!

As I was approaching the township of Yass, a wild yet windless thunderstorm blew in. I’ve never seen clouds move that fast, yet not a breath of wind – and it wasn’t even the right time of year for thunderstorms. It was also unseasonable warm that day. I’m not the most knowledgeable student of advanced cloud microphysics in the valley, but I do know that the role of clouds is one of the most uncertain areas in climate science; they’re hard to measure and, depending on altitude, droplet temperature and other factors, can play either a warming or a cooling role. Even the climate scientists don’t know exactly what’s going to happen. They only know it’s going to be bad. That’s even scarier. What’s next, I wonder? Icebergs falling from the sky?

I thought back to Book I of Aristotle’s Meteorology:


...clouds have often been observed moving with a great noise close to the earth, terrifying those who heard and saw them as portents of some catastrophe. Sometimes, too, when such clouds have been seen, without any noise, there follows a violent hailstorm, and the stones are of incredible size, and angular in shape.
My cowboy life is so happy and free
Out west where the laws don’t bother me
I take my troubles like a toy
I’m just a yodelling cowboy...

Open Letter to Xi Jinping

Xi,

I feel like you’re the only one I can really talk to, even though I don’t even know you. And I’m sorry if you’re far too busy running the People’s Republic of China to read this letter, but I believe it important to tell you how I feel, regardless.

I must confess, you are a fascinating man, and I believe you’re someone with whom I would genuinely enjoy conversing – ideally while sipping whiskey and smoking cigars, of course, if that ever again becomes possible. But I’m writing to you today not so much to express my personal admiration, nor to invite you over for a few drinks and a smoke. I am writing to you today to enlist your aid in diffusing tensions between our two nations.

No doubt it comes as no surprise that some idiot you’ve never heard of is writing to you today regarding this matter. Given the current level of misgovernance to which Australia is currently being subjected, and given the current level of needless political antipathy between Australia and China, I’m sure you can understand why I feel it necessary to write to you today. Additionally, the fact that I am now unemployable and shall soon again be made homeless is also compelling me to write to you today.

For the next few days, at least, I live in a small cottage in a sheep and wine region of south-eastern Australia. Yet I have no wine, and I’m running out of food. I only have a bag of rice and two eggs left. My landlord, Farmer Rob (no kidding, his name really is Rob), is over 65 and drinks a bottle of red every day at $41 a day. But I must admit it is good wine. In any case, I might have to help myself to one of his sheep tomorrow. I suppose I could still make green curry lamb with rice – but with no green curry, and no wine.

Wait a sec... I just remembered I still have 16 frozen vegetable dumplings left in the freezer. Hooray!

A forceful knock at the door.

I never thought I could get into so much trouble just from writing letters. Farmer Rob just called the cops on me. Some Pauline Hanson/Ronald McDonald look-a-like mutant clown cop and her excessively vigilante John Hughesque diminutive male Asian sidekick showed up on my doorstep just now. Farmer Rob has, according to his sacred Christian duty, informed the local police that he’s concerned for my welfare. How touching. Thank you, Farmer Rob, for being so thoughtful and looking out for me so diligently. I do so appreciate your concern ever so much. If only you could ever do the same for the land you stole and destroyed. You’re the one that needs help. You can come on over and fix my toilet though, if you ever need something useful to do.

Excuse me, Xi, but these constant interruptions, not to mention my current impoverished state, are preventing me from finishing this letter in a timely fashion. And my toilet really is broken. I also just ran out of toilet paper. But I don’t want to take up any more of your time with my personal problems, so I’ll get straight to the point.

I want my country back. I know, they’ll never give it up willingly. Yet keep in mind that the “they” is only a very small group of extremely wealthy people (Murdoch’s set) and their neofascist facilitatees – primarily, Prime Lump and Sergeant Potato Head. Yes, my country is run by a theocratic mendacious marketing manager who believes in “miracles”, assisted by his 80s-style Queensland cop sidekick who believes Australia is being invaded by left-wing African gangster Jihadists from New Zealand. I do apologise for this, Xi, but you must understand that what was once referred to as the “political class” in Australia no longer exists. Most of them are now dead or in prison, or forced into self-exile or early retirement, or relegated to the press gallery. That’s quite a subversive statement to be making, isn’t it? Yet that is the truth. I really should be more careful about what I say, I know. They’re always listening. I can’t do anything here without being spied on half to death. I suppose you’d expect that, to some extent, when living in a foreign nation, but not your own. But then the nation of Australia, as it is currently misrepresented by its current government, is not mine own. I reject it entirely. And I believe the vast majority of Australians now feel this way too. Again, I do apologise for this current state of affairs. However, I can assure you that work is now underway to solve this problem once and for all. Your patience, therefore, while we finally rectify this very difficult period in our nation’s history is much appreciated.

Rest assured, the year 2020 marks the end of Australia as you once knew it. That this end also happens to coincide with my departure from the Australian workforce is purely coincidental. But I’m not too worried about that. For you see I have a new guitar. Her name is Betty. She was made in China specifically for the Australian market. She is robust, efficient and responsive, yet delicate when required. I believe I’ll keep her. I suppose that makes sense. Most of the competent people I’ve worked with in Australia were originally from China – with one notable exception; but that was while working at UNSW, so that doesn’t count. Conversely, my most recent experience, in Canberra, working illegally and with no security clearances on state and federal government systems, will count. For it has been this latest experience, occurring at the tail end of a 23-year stint in the misinformation technology industry, that has finally forced my final exit from said industry – and in more ways than one.

Excuse me again, Xi, but I just learned that Charley Pride died today, due to complications related to Covid. I haven’t listened to Charley Pride for years. How does a man get to be this way? I just put some Charley Pride on. By the way, I don’t blame China for coronavirus. I’m no epidemiologist, but I do know that the origins of viruses can rarely be delimited to the sites of their initially reported outbreaks. I blame meat...and The Underwear Poisoner.

I just wish we had of known about it sooner.

And where’s the rest of the data?

Anyway, as I was saying, we all know that democracy, as it is presently practised in most present-day so-called democracies, is dead. We need something entirely new to replace it. Covid is our Chernobyl. Just take a look at the death tolls by country. And we all know that Communism, in its present CCP incarnation, has a very limited lifespan in China – as the middle class rise in the East and fall in the West, and while neoliberal democracies continue to disintegrate and collapse in upon themselves, and as China becomes the world’s largest economy. As both these lifespans are now coming to an end, a merger is inevitable. As surely as the continent of Australia shall some day merge with Asia, so too shall our two great civilisations coalesce into one to form the first truly global republic. We have too much freedom in some areas, you guys don’t have enough in others. We must merge and balance each other out. Mark my words, Xi, Australia will become China’s ally by 2028. We were allies once. There is no reason why we should not be so again. We joined forces once to defeat fascism. We can do it again – and this time finally. Fear and aggression will never dissuade us. We will eventually become one. It’s just a matter of time.

China, the world’s oldest continuous living civilisations; and Australia, the world’s oldest continuous living cultures. What could be better?

But in order to assemble this new republic into being, we must first put an end to all that authoritarian strong man shit, Xi – both from within and from without. The time for that style of political leadership has passed. This planet has experienced quite enough of it. And that’s not a request. That’s just the soon-to-be dominant global ethos. That may sound like so much wishful thinking (which I suppose it is), yet that must still stand as our ultimate goal.

They say I died on the beach in Singapore too far-sighted. However, I assure you I am still quite alive, and I’m really not that far-sighted. In fact, I’m slowly becoming near-sighted.

Xi, let me show you the real Chinas. I hate war but I do know a lot about it – the psychology and politics of war, not so much the practice of it. Maybe that’s why I hate it so much? And no, it’s not a love-hate relationship. I don’t believe in oversimplified dualistic phrases like that, and I don’t believe in relationships. I believe in co-existence and cooperation. I’m so tired of other people trying to force their master/whore relationships on me. We should be building flying cars and synthetic meat together. As it is, we’re neither building non-flying cars nor non-synthetic meat together. How is that not even not possible, I ask you? We cannot let ideological differences stand in our way, neither those of the political variety nor the philosophical, nor the religious.

Like you, Xi, I’m an anti-theocratic atheist with semi-spiritual animistic leanings. However, I do believe in the right of every person to practice whatever kind of kooky faith their into, so long as they keep it out of politics, and advertising and education. And I don’t care what it is.

But enough of that. More important to me than ideological issues or matters of faith are women – and one woman in particular. I fell in love with her while writing to her while she was in prison. She was falsely imprisoned in Iran for 804 days. She’s since been released – a true miracle for which I’m truly thankful (despite it taking 804 days longer than it should have) – but there is another problem: she’s married. Sadly, I feel it would be inappropriate for me to continue any form of correspondence with her given this knowledge. So I’ve since turned my attention to North Korea.

Excuse me once again, Xi, but I just learned that Doug Anthony also just died (not from Covid). As you are no doubt aware, Doug Anthony was the Australian Minister for Primary Industry during the late 1970s and early 80s. Not that it’s of too much significance, yet I thought it somewhat relevant to mention the coincidence of his passing, since during his ministership he did encourage and foster stronger and broader trade relations with Japan – even if some of that resulting trade also involved the exportation of uranium. Not that I’m comparing myself with the likes of Doug Anthony, but I also wish to encourage and foster stronger and broader trade relations with Japan – and China; indeed all nations – just not the uranium. Anyway, I’ll get back to Kylie and North Korea.

So since Kylie is now free, and since she’s already married to someone else, I am now at full liberty to offer my services to the Democratic People’s Republic of Korea. And in order to achieve ever-lasting peace and prosperity throughout the Asia-Pacific region, I’m more than willing to wed Kim Yo Jong – even though she’s already married to someone else. I need a strong confident Korean woman to whip me into shape (again), and North Korea needs to join the rest of the world by repurposing its military-industrial complex and restructuring its economy. I can help with that. And since Australia doesn’t want me, I’m sure you’ll agree the next most obvious place for me to be is North Korea...or perhaps Israel.

Don’t get me wrong, Australia is a lovely place, when it’s not burning, blanketed in smoke or under water. However, I’ve yet to reach the age of early retirement, and I’ve always longed to explore the Korean peninsula, both North and South. I can never be quite certain as to the precise reasons why, yet I’ve always believed it my destiny to end my days in a fully unified Korea, smoking hashish and writing amateurish Hyangga poetry on the summit of Mount Kumgang – after, of course, first fathering the ultimate warrior race of Austral-Korean Übermensch.

Right now you’re probably thinking to yourself, So why are you writing to me about this? Why don’t you write directly to Kim Yo Jong? Or Kim Jong-un? He is the Supreme Leader of North Korea, not I, and Kim Yo Jong is his sister. Quite right. I’m doing so because I believe a formal introduction from you would be more suitable under the circumstances, given the delicate nature of the subject matter and the personalities of the parties involved, not to mention the attendant geopolitical ramifications. Moreover, I am quite shy. Plus I’ve got quite a few open letters going at the moment and I’m already starting to grow weary of the form. Besides, I’d probably just end up causing yet more offence.

Just between you and me, Xi, I’ve always longed to make love to Kim, in ways unheard of, in places unthought of, and in positions unimaginable throughout all of eternity, that much is true. Yet I assure my proposal of marriage is also genuine and true. And I assure you also that my intentions are entirely honourable in every other respect. All unattempted humour aside, my love for Kim is real, and I do know her mind. She is an extraordinary yet very unhappy woman imprisoned in a politically arranged marriage she did not wish for. She wishes for nothing more than to escape her loveless and lifeless prison. I can see it in her eyes. Can you not see it also? Outwardly she projects an image of redoubtable strength and confidence, but in truth she appears to me at times a vulnerable and inexperienced young woman who has never truly known the true joy of true love – in such a way a woman such as herself simply must. Her expression is so gaunt, characterless and cruel, yet so unfathomably beautiful. Every time I see her I become exceedingly aroused, in every sense. I’m sorry, Xi, but I must have her, I simply must. But then I think back to all those Korean “comfort women” during World War II. Am I behaving just like a Japanese Imperial rapist too? Would she think as much of me for expressing my love in such a manner? I assure you that it is not my intent. Fuck it, I don’t speak Korean anyway.

Sorry, Xi. I’m not very good at this, am I? Do you not see now why an introduction from you is so requisite?

Yes, how could you dare not think for a moment that I would not wish to become embroiled in the most interesting problem to date in all of geopolitical history? Trump (The Rapist in Chief), being a plagiarist and an egomaniacal profiteering opportunist, recognised this too. But sadly he was also a corrupt moronic psychopath and full of shit. And although he’s now gone (kind of), his dismal legacy still remains. And although I can appreciate the threat still posed, especially with all the evil clowns and arseheads still at large, I must say your militarist and authoritarian tendencies do tend to worry me somewhat – as do those of the Democratic People’s Republic of Korea. I’m trying to move away from all that silly nonsense. I’m gearing up for a real war – opening up government and repurposing and reprovisioning the military to combat the causes and effects of global heating. I’m not living through another Cold War, especially while I’m still living through the “War on Drugs”, the “War on Terror” and now the War on Truth. So I’ve decided to defect to North Korea. Yes, from the Korean peninsula shall we defend our Chinese comrades to the end, by disarming them all. Together we shall bring ever-lasting peace throughout the Asia-Pacific region, and thence the entire world. Global disarmament! We shall not allow them to socially engineer their own mutually assured destruction. We have a bigger and more dangerous enemy to fight: The Underwear Poisoner, an existential threat that we can only defeat by joining forces.

And since Kylie is unavailable, and since Dolly Parton refuses to bless my courtship of Sarah – which I have since commenced nonetheless – and given that I have no other ongoing romantic interests, I believe it makes perfect sense that Kim and I wed, geopolitically speaking at least. Do you not agree?

To be perfectly honest, Xi, I’d much rather be with Sarah and not be forced to engage in any of this silly nonsense. But given the current situation, and since you leave me with little choice, here’s my plan: Jump a slow boat to Nampo; wed Kim in a lavish traditional North Korean-style ceremony, with much soju and much hongeo; honeymoon for about three months on a remote tropical island in the Pacific; make love to Kim religiously, while she teaches me to speak Korean and Russian; return to North Korea to take up a low-level functionary post in Kim Jong-un’s administration; patiently await an invitation to visit Moscow to meet with The Underwear Poisoner; infiltrate his inner circle, with Kim as my guide; get invited to cocaine-fuelled oligarchical orgies; leave briefcase under the bed and walk away (casually). Too easy.

Don’t worry, I’ve done this kind of thing before.

That’s all probably just another one of my crazy pipe dreams, I know. Besides, I’m sure Kim has much better taste in men and would never agree to such a foolhardy enterprise, especially with such a scummy kind of guy like me.

But then how could I dare not to dream as much, given the current state of affairs?

If it were not for the deterioration in relations between Australia and China, perhaps things would be different? One can only speculate. Either way, “either a man will learn nothing at all or he will learn only what he already knows.” That does seem to be the general way with this current administration, does it not?

They don’t like that I’m writing to you. They see me as a traitor to the Great White Imperialist Cause of Rampant Militarism and Overly Centralised Wealth Accumulation. They treat me like a redefective spy for the CCP. I’ve never even been to China – unless you count that visa run to Hong Kong back in the late 90s. I didn’t even leave the airport. Now that I look back, I should have defected to China while I had the chance and lived over there for a while. But I was way too preoccupied with far too many other matters at the time. I love China and Chinese culture, however I don’t think I could ever live under Communist party rule (unless I were the Supreme Leader). I lived under the Maduro regime for two years in Venezuela. Maduroism isn’t really Communist, I know. Still, the trauma suffered during those two miserable years of free Spanish lessons still debilitates me to this day. I was lucky I got out alive. But I mostly blame The Underwear Poisoner for that. The last five years of accumulated trauma suffered under Australian neofascism, however, has been even worse. Maybe I should defect to China. Or perhaps not. I’m afraid if I do I’ll eventually get arrested for saying the wrong thing and sent off to one of those vocational training camps. Free Mandarin lessons! At least maybe then they could cure me of my long-standing hatred of China. Or perhaps not. These days anyone who refuses to hate China is seen as a Communist sympathiser. We’re going back to the bad old McCarthyism days. It’s by design, I’m sure of it. The neofascists are deliberately forcing China into a military alliance with The Underwear Poisoner. And then we’ll become even more paranoid and respond with yet more silliness (more hypersonic missile purchases and gunboat diplomacy probably), and then in another ten months or so we’ll all be at war again. Third time’s the charm. Yet more ternary clichés.

Well I for one say no more. No more ternary clichés! And no more war, of any kind.

That is why, since no one else cares to, I’ve taken the liberty of addressing each one of your fourteen grievances against Australia personally, some idiot you’ve never heard of though that I am. And I have also included fourteen grievances of my own, which I have phrased somewhat light-heartedly as “demands”, and which I expect you to address personally in a similar manner. Additionally, I’ve included fourteen things I like about China, since we’re always supposed to say something nice about someone before criticising them.

I’ve also taken the liberty of altering some of the grammar – purely for the sake of clarity – without, hopefully, altering any of the original sense or meaning of the transcript. And when I say transcript I mean your original English transcript, not the Daily Mail condensed Engrish rendering.

I have addressed each item in red below.


Fourteen Things China Doesn’t Like About Australia

  1. Foreign investments and acquisitions blocked on opaque national security grounds and in contravention of ChAFTA [China–Australia Free Trade Agreement]. Since 2018 more than 10 Chinese investment projects have been rejected by Australia, citing ambiguous and unfounded “national security concerns,” and placing restrictions on areas like infrastructure, agriculture and animal husbandry.
    The small dog barks the loudest.
  2. The decision to ban Huawei Technologies and ZTE from the 5G network over unfounded national security concerns; and doing the bidding of the US by lobbying other countries to do the same.
    As we all know, 5G causes fatal brain tumours in children, kills puppies and kittens instantly and spreads coronavirus all over the place. After an internal investigation into how these decisions were reached, an impartial and fact-based re-evaluation shall be made. I’ve already moved on to GPRS anyway.
  3. Foreign interference legislation targeted at China, in the absence of any evidence of interference.
    This is another by-product of Australia’s traditional racist and xenophobic attitude in general. For centuries, other supposedly friendlier nations have been more active in interfering in “Australia’s politics”. A government that formulates foreign policy that is fundamentally racist and culturally bigoted is bound to not only harm its own vital economic interests and diplomatic ties, but also leaves itself vulnerable to foreign interference from other more malign sources. This legislation will be revised. Our good friends the Canadians may be able to help us out with some of that.
  4. Politicisation and stigmatisation of the normal exchanges and cooperation between China and Australia, and creating barriers and imposing restrictions, including the revocation of visas for Chinese scholars.
    Lump is our Trump. I assure you, Xi, once Lump is gone normal exchanges and cooperation, in all forums, between China and Australia shall resume.
  5. Acting as a proxy for the US by calling for an international independent inquiry into the Covid-19 virus, echoing similar recent US attacks on China.
    Unlike some of my contemporaries, I am capable of discerning the difference between laying blame for being unable to the contain the spread of a new virus and investigating its origins. People often confuse investigations into the origins of outbreaks with the assessment of their responses to them. China did a better job than the U.S (initially at least). Why don’t we call for a separate investigation into why the United States has the highest number of infections and deaths? The WHO has separately convened a global study of the origins, so I think we know what Lump’s game is: “I’m still with stupid” cretin-created conspiracy theory puppet shows and childish tit for tat nonsense. But that’s what happens whenever you leave the paranoia-driven b-grade belligerent boy’s club bureaucrats in charge. The general populous on both sides suffer, not them.
  6. The incessant wanton interference in China’s Xinjiang, Hong Kong and Taiwan affairs; spearheading the crusade against China in certain multilateral forums.
    I believe no nation has the right to interfere in the affairs of any other nation, unless there is a clear violation of human rights occurring. Regarding Hong Kong, there’s not much I can say, other than that I’m extremely disappointed China has gone back on its word. But given the advent of The Rapist in Chief, I can at least understand the motivation. And I can console myself with the knowledge that the democratic reforms China will undoubtedly undergo in coming decades will also apply broadly and equally to Hong Kong (once we curb your militarist and authoritarian tendencies). With respect to Taiwan, the people of Taiwan shall determine their own fate. Some would argue they already have. I can understand how China would wish to reclaim by force the territories severed from it in the past, but the region has changed quite significantly since then, and the island of Taiwan no less so. It’s no longer the year 1683. Force is the loser’s way. The only solution here is a diplomatic one. There is only one Chinas. You have my full support on that, Xi. Besides, we need to take the Philippines first. Regarding Xinjiang, I only know what I read in the press: arbitrary detentions and degrading treatment inflicted upon Uyghurs and people from other ethnic minorities, as well as systematic violations of their freedom of religion or belief (as if China is the only nation guilty of that), forced labour camps, cultural “genocide”, etc. Australia tried all that a few decades back (some would argue they’re still trying it), but it only ever created more problems. And even if you do manage to kill them all, they still come back to haunt you later on, and in ever greater numbers. Genocide is like that, it never really goes away. However, I do understand that wanton interference is rarely helpful under any circumstances. Warranted influence is always preferable. We must all accept some warranted influence at times. China would not enjoy the affluence it does now without the influence of others. And with respect to “spearheading the crusade,” Australia shall be spearheading no such crusades in future. Australia will be focusing on restoring and strengthening its relations with China, and indeed with all its trading partners.
  7. The first non-littoral nation to make a statement on the South China Sea to the United Nations.
    I have to say, Australia has every right to be concerned about China’s activities in the South China Sea, just as China, and all other nations, have every right to be concerned about every other nation’s activities in the South China Sea. However, I do like the idea of building artificial islands. I just wish we could do it together – especially seeing as how most of the non-artificial ones will all be underwater soon. I love islands. I’m not so in love with the idea of non-freedom or militias, however. Why can’t we all set aside our petty differences, adopt the Antarctic treaty model, abide by international court rulings and start building artificial islands together? And why can’t we also start repairing all the existing islands, which will all be under water soon if we don’t?
  8. Siding with the US’ anti-China campaign and spreading disinformation imported from the US around China’s efforts at containing COVID-19.
    Yes, the blatant hypocrisy and malevolent spite here truly beggars belief. But this is more of a Trump thing. Trump is now gone, and Lump will be gone soon too. No Trump, no Lump.
  9. The latest legislation scrutinising agreements with foreign governments, targeting China and specifically aimed at torpedoing the state of Victoria’s participation in the Belt & Road initiative.
    This one worries me too. I like driving around Australia, except in Victoria. Victoria has some of the worst roads, and drivers, in all of Australia. Australians are just so shit at building roads, except in Queensland, but especially in Victoria. I can’t tell you how many times I’ve come close to death on Victorian roads, so I won’t. But I can tell you that Victoria’s participation in the Belt & Road initiative will go ahead, in one form or another, a few months after the next federal election – once all that revised legislation is enacted, and all those corrupt opportunists are out of the way. These current difficulties are merely temporary delays.

    Which think tank? There’s more than a few – mostly group think tanks whose primary purpose it is to push second-hand USUK arms sales and an inevitable war with China. The Australian Strategic Policy Institute (ASPI) being the main offender (-35.307801319129936, 149.13582123568776) – an antiquated vestige of war-mongering evil from the Howard era. Their main policy being to stoke fear, promote the sale of weapons and turn major population centres into military targets. But then most Australians are all for a war with China. They’ve been raised to believe it’s inevitable. You must understand, Xi, that most Australians have been force-fed a steady diet of anti-China propaganda for most of their lives. China is only ever reported on from an adversarial stance in their press, so necessarily they have a negative view of China. It’s going to take some time to educate them with the truth – which, as we both know, is far more complex. They see the whole of China, or the CCP, as one single unified entity of supreme all-powerful evil. Ignorance, hypocrisy, fear, aggression, greed and corruption are the true evils here, as always.

    Yes, they do that to Australian journalists’ homes too.   12. Thinly veiled allegations of Chinese cyber attacks without any evidence.

Remember, they want war. They profit from it.

The Law of Penguins, and Their Poo

The Law of Penguins is long, boring and abstruse. It is best expressed to the unilluminated in the following conversational form:

Young girl: What is the Law of Penguins?

Old man: The Law of Penguins is a law that prescribes how penguins avoid their own poo.

Young girl: How do penguins avoid their own poo?

Old man: Well, there are no penguins, and there is no penguin poo, so there’s no poo for penguins to avoid, since neither penguins nor their poo exist. I hope that answers your question.

Young girl: No, it doesn’t.

A Night at the Toowoomba Showgrounds

My first night as a forced early retired homeless person was spent at the Toowoomba Showgrounds. It was truly a magical experience. I slept in my car under the big metal windmill – the recently refurbished ten-metre Comet B-Pattern windmill. It pumps no water, of course. Its presence is purely for ornamental and heritage preservation purposes. Yet it is still truly magnificent.

It’s a warm summer afternoon a few days before Christmas. The showgrounds are for the most part vacant. There’s only five other happy campers, including myself. I park beside the windmill and give it a thorough inspection. I won’t bore you with the technical details. It’s a big metal windmill, that’s all you need to know. It stands on a grassy slope overlooking the main entrance. Here I sit with a bottle of whiskey while surveying the scene. The shade of a large oak tree shields me from the burning late-afternoon sun. A few people walk past along the road below. They wave. I hide the whiskey. I wave back. Santa Claus drives past. I wave. He’s wearing shiny red shorts and driving a horse-drawn wooden cart loaded with presents. He waves back. I raise my glass and take a sip. In the distance I can see the grand hilltop houses that seem to float atop the leafy canopies of the few remaining eucalyptus trees. That’s probably where Santa’s headed. I take another sip while savouring the last few moments of relative blissful silence.

Unbeknownst to me before arriving, my stay at the Toowoomba Showgrounds came with a complimentary fireworks practice session – in preparation for some upcoming festive event, I gather. I look up at the windmill, its broad steel windwheel rotating majestically in the cool evening breeze. I’ve never thought about it before, but I suppose windmills do look a bit like comets. I close my eyes and listen to the steady rhythmic clanking of it’s mechanical inner workings. I then begin to imagine what a real comet would sound like, if it were ever capable of making sound. Then the fireworks begin.

The fireworks practise session went off splendidly and coincided nicely with my current state of mind. After such a decisive end to a gruelling 23-year stint in the misinformation technology industry, some celebratory fireworks action was indeed well in order.

As the whirling, whizzing rockets burst and boom above my head, I raise my glass in a final farewell toast to my pointless waste of a useless life.

Farewell, fatally dispirited fellow developers!
Farewell, non-technical technical project mismanagers!
Farewell, do-nothing know-nothing CTOs!
Farewell, mendacious marketing fuckwits!
Farewell, apathetic hands-off product owners!
Farewell, desktop-only brochureware redesigners!
Farewell, illiterate and banal copywriters!
Farewell, predatory and parasitic recruiters!

Yes, I bid you all a fond farewell, you poor enslaved suburban office hicks. I’d rather live in my car under a big metal windmill than work with any of you ever again. May you all be damned for all of eternity for turning the internets into a stinking pile of fascist advertising garbage, and may future generations forgive me for contributing to their final ruin – not that I expect they ever will.

¡Salud!

I’m So Glad You Weren’t There to Hear It

Why are you so afraid? It’s just music, with no words and no political messaging. Why is that so threatening to you? Is it me, personally? Personally, I have no other agenda other than the perfection of the thing in itself. However, if you try to hinder me again I will become the very thing in and of itself – everything you fear the most.

Recently I rediscovered an irregular guitar tuning: seconds and sixes. I have also recently rediscovered the perfect secluded beach – so secluded I had trouble finding it again myself. You can’t see it from the road; it’s hidden behind ’s a small grove of Casuarina trees (Casuarina equisetifolia) to your right as you turn one of the many bends along the highway – or to your left, depending on which direction you’re travelling. This bend in the road has a very distinct and permanent musical association for me – yet for you it does not and is therefore indistinguishable from the many other bends in the road. There’s an outcrop of boulders concealing a pathway through the trees. A few metres along the path there’s a near-vertical ten-metre rock-faced drop to the beach below. Last night, just after sunset, and with Betty by my side, we clambered down the rockface together to reacquaint ourselves with the rare pleasures of these recent rediscoveries.

A waxing crescent Moon in Pisces looms expectantly above the mountains, Saturn and Jupiter conjoined at her nether tip. I picked a good time. Betty and I shall be accompanied this evening by a celestial alignment that has not occurred for over 400 years. Not that that’s of any great interest to you. You’re probably more interested in the beach – which is, quite simply, perfect. I rarely often trade in superlatives, but on just this one occasion no other word shall suffice. It really is the most perfect beach imaginable – a crescent-shaped stretch of soft white sand, a few palm trees, a calm shallow sea, the soothing sound of waves gently lapping, and at the far side a massive Casuarina tree. This tree truly is quite large, both for its species and location. It seems to grow directly from the rocks themselves, which enclose the beach at either end. Its broad muscular trunk leans forward at a 54-degree angle towards the sea and its branches extend far beyond the shoreline. Just how this tree grew so large has always puzzled me, considering the rather harsh and forbidding ground in which it has taken root. There’s also a freshwater spring that sometimes flows from the rockface behind the tree. Perhaps this is in part attributable?

The dark-mirrored sea sparkles with reflected starlight, as I take my seat centre stage on the fine white sands. With Betty’s warm amazique body close to mine, I begin by initiating some tentative tuneful foreplay. To my extreme relief she responds accordingly. The acoustics of this littoral amphitheatre seem to agree with her. Betty begins to open up for me. Betty now opens up for me to such a state and to such a degree that she begins to play me. I can’t really describe to you what she plays – nor do I care to. Gentlemen never tell, and all that you know. All I can tell you is what I think about while she plays. I first think about the Jupiter and Saturn conjunction occurring right above my head. I then think about how I’m going to write about this. I also think about the rhythm of the waves, how they double up every sixth beat and how to me this always sounds like time itself.

Why must I go to such lengths to escape you? Just because I occasionally write and play a bit of music that gives you the right to stalk and terrorise me, does it? Spy on me and deprive me of a life, I deprive you all, including myself. I don’t write for money or perform, ever. And I sure don’t willingly share with stalkers. And you won’t let me work, since I openly identify as an asexual anti-technotheocratic anarcho-naturalist. Or is it because I’ve had too much sex or did too many drugs when I was younger? Which I really don’t think I have. I really should have had a lot more sex and done a lot more drugs when I was younger, to be quite honest. In fact, when I think about all the sex and drugs I’ve missed out on over the years it makes me quite angry. But it’s still worth it. Nature conspires sometimes at seemingly random moments to create real magic. You have no idea how good it felt to play and hear, and nor shall you ever – something quite unique that could never be played again, even if I, or Betty, cared to.

And you all know who you have to thank for that.

Somewhere near Palm Cove, Queensland, Australia, 2020

Christmas in Mount Isa

They say you’re not a real Australian until you’ve visited Mount Isa, the rodeo capital of Australia. Now that I’m here, I can say I fully agree with that statement.

I’m spending Christmas day alone again – but no weed or wine or McDonald’s this year, just a bottle of Scotch. I haven’t made too much progress, have I? Except maybe on the Clydesdale: saw one in Toowoomba.

But this is exactly how I prefer to celebrate Christmas – sitting alone outside my eighties-style motel room, smoking cigarettes and sipping whiskey, watching a Black-shouldered kite circle high above the Hard Times Mining Company headframe.

This place is so dead. I wish the rodeo were on. I’ve been here two days already waiting for the floods up north to subside. Tomorrow I’m going to try to drive up to Katherine in one day. This place is so dead. Reminds me of Tamworth, the country music capital of Australia – dead every other day of the year but for the few that supposedly characterise it.

About the only thing I knew about Mount Isa before I got here was that Lindy Chamberlain was living here when she got Lindyed. Appropriate, I suppose. They say you’re not a real Australian until you’ve been Lindyed.

Since the rodeo’s not on, and since I have no one to talk to, I begin to imagine a conversation between a rodeo cowboy and Lindy Chamberlain. They’re discussing the upcoming state of a very different kind of rodeo.

Lindy: Well, at least we know who they are now. So this is really going to happen?

Cowboy: Oh yeah. They’ll all be sitting on my stockyard rail pretty soon. Rodeo’s coming to town. Time to round up all the evil clowns.

Lindy: Like a rhinestone cowboy?

Cowboy: Exactly. The ultimate star-spangled rodeo.

Lindy: Yeehaw!
